There\xe2\x80\x99s no excuse.\xe2\x80\x9d'
b'While the outburst was hardly unexpected for Harden, who is now averaging an N.B.A.-leading 34.8 points a game, the Rockets\xe2\x80\x99 personnel situation made it stand out. Paul has been out with an injured hamstring since Dec. 20 and Gordon has been out with an injured knee since Dec. 29. Houston\xe2\x80\x99s injury report then took on what seemed like a crippling blow earlier on Monday when it was revealed that Capela, the team\xe2\x80\x99s center \xe2\x80\x94 and the most frequent recipient of Harden\xe2\x80\x99s assists \xe2\x80\x94 would be out for four to six weeks as a result of ligament damage in his right thumb.'
b'That list of injuries left Harden starting alongside the forgettable quartet of P.J. Tucker, Nene, Austin Rivers and Danuel House Jr. No matter, as Harden joined Kemba Walker as the only players to score more than half of their team\xe2\x80\x99s points in a game this season.'
b'Harden was hot from the start, setting a Rockets record with 36 points in the first half, and he succeeded all game with his typical combination of 3-pointers (6 for 15) and free-throws (17 for 18). b'The last time Harden scored fewer than 30 points was Dec. 11 in Houston\xe2\x80\x99s win over the Portland Trail Blazers, and he just barely missed the feat that night, with 29 points on 10 of 21 shooting. b'Chamberlain had 30-point streaks, of 20, 25, 31 and 65 games in his career, according to Basketball-Reference.com. The longest one, which came during the 1961-62 season, is likely an unbreakable record, but it comes with an amusing footnote: In Chamberlain\xe2\x80\x99s last game before the streak started, he was held to 28 points in a loss to Bill Russell\xe2\x80\x99s Boston Celtics. When the streak finally ended more than three months later, Chamberlain was held to 26 points \xe2\x80\x94 in a loss to Russell\xe2\x80\x99s Celtics.'
b'As it currently stands, though, Harden does not appear to have a foil that can be his version of Russell, so there is no telling when this streak will end.'

b'By Scott Cacciola'
b'LOS ANGELES \xe2\x80\x94 Vast upheaval within the Los Angeles Lakers organization continued on Friday afternoon when the team announced that Luke Walton was stepping down as coach.'
b'The Lakers said in a statement that Walton and the team had \xe2\x80\x9cmutually agreed to part ways,\xe2\x80\x9d without elaborating. The news came three days after Magic Johnson, the team\xe2\x80\x99s president for basketball operations, made the surprise announcement that he was resigning so he could devote more time to his business interests.'
b'Walton, 39, was in his third season with the Lakers, who were expected to vie for a playoff spot after signing LeBron James, a four-time N.B.A. most valuable player, to a four-year, $154 million contract last July. Instead, the Lakers scuffled to a 37-45 record after months of general dysfunction and momentum-sapping injuries. They finished 10th in the Western Conference, well out of playoff position.'
b'The N.B.A.\xe2\x80\x99s postseason will start Saturday but without the Lakers, whose postseason drought is now at six seasons. Not even the celebrated addition of James could salvage this one, but he missed significant time with a groin injury. And even when he was on the court, he appeared detached from his teammates as weeks of misery mounted.'
b'The Lakers are fraught with problems. When Johnson announced that he was quitting this week, he indicated that he had been planning to fire Walton and that he had the support of Jeanie Buss, the team\xe2\x80\x99s controlling owner, to go forward with the move. But then Johnson resigned \xe2\x80\x94 in part, he said, because he could not go through with affecting someone\xe2\x80\x99s \xe2\x80\x9clivelihood.\xe2\x80\x9d'
b'Hours later, after the Lakers had closed out their season with a loss to the Portland Trail Blazers, Walton said that he was looking forward to an eventful summer with the team in hopes of making improvements. Now he is gone, too, though he may not be unemployed for long.'
b'The Sacramento Kings immediately responded to Friday\xe2\x80\x99s news by reaching out to Walton\xe2\x80\x99s representatives to arrange an interview for their coaching vacancy, according to two people familiar with Sacramento\xe2\x80\x99s plans who were not authorized to discuss them publicly. b'Steve Kerr, the coach of the Golden State Warriors, expressed his support for Walton, one of his former assistants.'
b'\xe2\x80\x9cIn this job, as a coach in the N.B.A., you are 100 percent dependent on your circumstances: the strength of your organization, the momentum, unity,\xe2\x80\x9d Kerr told reporters in Oakland, Calif. \xe2\x80\x9cEverything has to be in good order, because if it\xe2\x80\x99s not, as we have witnessed with the Lakers, then there\xe2\x80\x99s going to be casualties, and usually the coach is the first one.\xe2\x80\x9d'
b'He added: \xe2\x80\x9cThey\xe2\x80\x99re losing one of the best humans in the N.B.A. They\xe2\x80\x99re losing a guy who knows the game as well as anybody I\xe2\x80\x99ve met. They\xe2\x80\x99re losing somebody who players believe in.\xe2\x80\x9d'
b'Walton, the son of the Hall of Fame center Bill Walton, was working with an ill-conceived roster that lacked depth, defense and perimeter shooting. Still, the pressure was on him before the season even began. Once the Lakers got off to a slow start, Johnson chastised Walton in a closed-door meeting, raising speculation that Walton was already on the hot seat.'
b'Questions about Walton\xe2\x80\x99s job security persisted throughout the season as he shuffled rotations and lineups, searching for solutions that never materialized.'
b'Walton refused to make excuses \xe2\x80\x94 publicly, he was a voice of unwavering optimism amid a sea of discontent \xe2\x80\x94 but it hardly helped that the Lakers were troubled by injuries, especially at point guard.'
b'Then there was James, who had been incredibly durable in his 16-year career. But during the Lakers\xe2\x80\x99 Christmas Day game against the Warriors, he limped off the court with a strained groin and missed the next 17 games. Without him, the Lakers struggled. The hope was that they could regain their footing once he returned, but he was not the cure-all anyone imagined. The Lakers continued to lose with James back in the lineup, even though he said he had \xe2\x80\x9cactivated\xe2\x80\x9d himself for a playoff push.'
b'It had become clear by then, however, that the Lakers did not have any discernible chemistry, especially after Johnson and Rob Pelinka, their general manager, tried and failed to acquire the All-Star center Anthony Davis from the New Orleans Pelicans ahead of February\xe2\x80\x99s trade deadline. (It was no coincidence, perhaps, that Davis and James shared an agent, Rich Paul.) The Lakers were willing to send the Pelicans several of their promising young players, including Kyle Kuzma, Brandon Ingram and Lonzo Ball, but were rebuffed in their attempts to swing a blockbuster deal.'
b'The result was a team that seemed distracted at best and fractured at worst. Before long, the Lakers were officially eliminated from playoff contention. James did not dress for the final six games of the season.'
b'Walton, who spent most of his 10-year N.B.A. playing career with the Lakers, winning two championships as a reserve forward, was hired as their coach in 2016 after two seasons as an assistant with the Warriors. In 2015-16, he began the season as the Warriors\xe2\x80\x99 interim coach while Kerr recovered from debilitating back issues, and guided the team to a 39-4 record, which included a league-record 24 straight wins to start the season.'
b'It was certainly an achievement, but the Warriors were coming off a championship and primed to excel. With the Lakers, Walton was trying to build something. Now, that vast project \xe2\x80\x94 however onerous \xe2\x80\x94 will continue without him.'

A recent injury aside, that is still expected to be the Duke star Zion Williamson. A bottom three finish would also give the Knicks a 40 percent chance at a top three pick.'

Despite their win, they look likely to grab a bottom three spot, probably alongside the Phoenix Suns (11-50) and Cleveland Cavaliers (14-46). But the Chicago Bulls are looming, two games \xe2\x80\x9cbetter\xe2\x80\x9d than the Cavs.'
b'The league actually changed the draft lottery percentages this season in an effort to cut down on tanking, particularly after the 76ers went on a multiyear losing period of terrible play that got them several top picks. A year ago, the worst record offered a full 25 percent chance at No. 1, with the second and third worst teams getting 20 and 16 percent chances.'
b'Lee has been the Knicks\xe2\x80\x99 consensus No. 1 fan for years, sitting courtside and not infrequently interacting with players on both teams. Perhaps most infamously, in 1994, he jawed with the Pacers\xe2\x80\x99 Reggie Miller in a conference finals game. Miller went on to the lead the Pacers to victory, drawing a \xe2\x80\x9cThanks a Lot Spike\xe2\x80\x9d headline from The New York Daily News.'
b'Jackson and Lee have a history as well, with Jackson appearing in \xe2\x80\x9cDo the Right Thing,\xe2\x80\x9d \xe2\x80\x9cSchool Daze,\xe2\x80\x9d \xe2\x80\x9cJungle Fever\xe2\x80\x9d and \xe2\x80\x9cMo Better Blues.\xe2\x80\x9d They are also both alumni of Morehouse College.'
b'In this age of smartphones, there\xe2\x80\x99s a good chance that those at the Oscars who cared already knew the Knicks score, perhaps including Lee.'
b'That wasn\xe2\x80\x99t the case in 1976, when Elliott Gould, presenting the award for best editing, alerted the audience that Indiana had won the men\xe2\x80\x99s basketball national championship, 86-68. \xe2\x80\x9cI listened to the score before we went out to make the presentation,\xe2\x80\x9d he told Grantland. \xe2\x80\x9cLiterally in the wings, there was a radio there.\xe2\x80\x9d'
b'By the way, along with his co-writers, Lee won on Sunday, his first competitive Oscar. There is no evidence that \xe2\x80\x9cThe Ballad of Buster Scruggs\xe2\x80\x9d or the other nominees engaged in any tanking.'

b'By Kelly Whiteside'
b'Knicks Coach David Fizdale pulled at the edge of his graying beard as he dissected his team\xe2\x80\x99s latest blowout loss. Leading a team that is now 10-42, the worst record in the N.B.A., Fizdale has had to search hard for traces of sunshine.'
b'As he answered questions from reporters at a recent postgame news conference, the frames of his trademark glasses looked as broken as the franchise itself. The damaged black frames were held together by a glop of glue; Fizdale had cracked them earlier in the season.'
b'It is easy to say now, but with 30 games remaining the Knicks seem to have been lost from the start. They began the season with the youngest roster in the N.B.A., with an average age of less than 24.5 years old. Development became the mantra with Fizdale, who in his first season as the Knicks head coach has frequently referred to his players as \xe2\x80\x9ckids.\xe2\x80\x9d Inexperience, a revolving-door rotation, and the absence of Kristaps Porzingis \xe2\x80\x94 the star forward who has been out injured since February 2018 \xe2\x80\x94 compounded the losing.'
b'Now, after last week\xe2\x80\x99s trade that sent Porzingis to the Dallas Mavericks ended any hope that he might return to save the season, the Knicks could be in danger of finishing with the worst record in franchise history. The low mark was a 17-65 record during the 2014-15 season. They have lost 13 in a row, 25 of the last 27 and a franchise-record 14 consecutive games at home. Not surprisingly, they were 27th in the league in offensive rating and 28th in defensive rating entering Monday night\xe2\x80\x99s games.'
b'Of course, Knicks fans have become inured to the losing \xe2\x80\x94 this will be the team\xe2\x80\x99s sixth consecutive season without a winning record. Other than the 2012-13 season, when the Knicks reached the Eastern Conference semifinals, it has been nearly two decades since the team advanced beyond the first round of the playoffs.'
b'Newcomers like Kevin Knox, Mitchell Robinson and Allonzo Trier may be the future, but injuries and inconsistency have marred the present. Knox, the 6-foot-9 forward chosen ninth over all in last year\xe2\x80\x99s draft, is one of the youngest players in the league, at 19. In December he earned Eastern Conference Rookie of the Month honors, but his 37.1 shooting percentage needs to improve.'
b'The Knicks took a gamble on the 7-foot-1 Robinson when they selected him in the second round of June\xe2\x80\x99s draft, 36th over all. He was the only player in last year\xe2\x80\x99s draft who did not play in college, overseas or in the N.B.A.\xe2\x80\x99s developmental league. Instead, Robinson took a year off from organized basketball after high school to get ready for the draft.'
b'Trier, a 6-foot-5 guard, went undrafted after three seasons at Arizona, but his early impressive play led to a two-year, $7 million deal with the Knicks.'
b'The Knicks\xe2\x80\x99 front office has been lauded for its savvy picks in last year\xe2\x80\x99s draft and its recent acquisition of reclamation projects. That acumen will be tested in June. The Knicks, who own a first-round draft pick, will have the chance to select an impact player with their winning-by-losing approach.'
b'The more they lose, the better their chances are of landing Duke\xe2\x80\x99s Zion Williamson or another highly coveted prospect. Still, it is not a slam dunk \xe2\x80\x94 even if the Knicks fail to win 20 games this year. Being the worst team in the N.B.A. used to provide a greater advantage in the draft lottery. Because the league changed the rule to deter teams from tanking, the bottom three teams now share the same 14 percent odds of winning the No. 1 pick. Previously, the worst team held a 25 percent chance.'
b'\xe2\x80\x9cObviously, you always want to win. Every game we play we\xe2\x80\x99re trying to win,\xe2\x80\x9d Fizdale has said.'
b'But what if the Knicks actually did start winning, boosted by the three players acquired in the Porzingis trade with Dallas? The Knicks gained the promising guard Dennis Smith Jr., who was a first-round draft pick in 2017, and the expiring contracts of the veterans DeAndre Jordan and Wesley Matthews, plus two future first-round picks. Porzingis, Tim Hardaway Jr., Courtney Lee and Trey Burke were shipped to the Mavericks.'
b'The Knicks\xe2\x80\x99 newcomers knew only a few of the team\xe2\x80\x99s offensive plays before making their debut against Memphis on Sunday, with Smith Jr. and Jordan starting. Both made standout plays early. Smith scored his first basket on a drive into the lane with an up-and-under layup and added another in a fast-break opportunity. Jordan registered a block, followed by an alley-oop dunk off an assist from Smith. All this competent basketball made some Knicks fans nervous, leading to some angst-ridden gallows humor on social media.'
b'The Knicks held on for the loss, 96-84.'
b'With Smith and Jordan in the starting lineup, the Knicks have continued their season theme of roster roulette. Fizdale has stitched together 57 five-man lineups that have played 10 or more minutes together this season. But of those groups, only five lineups have played 50 or more minutes together.'
b'Consider center Enes Kanter, who started 23 games but lost his starting job as the team decided to focus on developing its younger players. He did not go quietly to the end of the bench. \xe2\x80\x9cI\xe2\x80\x99ll go out and do my job and help my team win,\xe2\x80\x9d he said in late December. \xe2\x80\x9cIf we\xe2\x80\x99re winning, it\xe2\x80\x99s good. But if we\xe2\x80\x99re losing it\xe2\x80\x99s a problem. If this adjustment is going to get us a win, cool. But if not, there\xe2\x80\x99s a problem.\xe2\x80\x9d'
b'But lately the most vocal cheer at Madison Square Garden has been, \xe2\x80\x9cWe want Kanter!\xe2\x80\x9d as he sits on the bench. After four consecutive games in which he did not play, Kanter entered the game against Dallas last week, went to his knees and kissed the midcourt Garden logo. He explained later that he wanted to show his love for the fans since it could be one of his final games as a Knick, with the trade deadline looming.'
b'In the second quarter against Memphis on Sunday, Fizdale looked down the bench and called for \xe2\x80\x9cDennis,\xe2\x80\x9d referring to the newly acquired point guard Dennis Smith Jr. Kanter, however, heard \xe2\x80\x9cEnes\xe2\x80\x9d and started for the scorer\xe2\x80\x99s table until he was stopped by the assistant coach Keith Smart.'
b'\xe2\x80\x9cHe wanted to run all the way to the scorer\xe2\x80\x99s table, make it a bigger spectacle,\xe2\x80\x9d Fizdale said. But the damage, as it is with the Knicks, was already done.'
